## MANDATORY: Use Sourcegraph MCP for Code Search

You have Sourcegraph MCP tools. You MUST use them INSTEAD OF Grep, Glob, and bash grep/rg/find for ALL code search.

- Instead of Grep -> use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_keyword_search`
- Instead of Glob -> use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_list_files`
- For symbol definitions -> use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_go_to_definition`
- For all references -> use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_find_references`
- For complex code understanding questions, use `mcp__sourcegraph__sg_deepsearch`

Repository filter for sg_keyword_search: `repo:^github.com/sg-benchmarks/kubernetes--8c9c67c0$ QUERY`

If you catch yourself reaching for Grep or Glob to *find* code, STOP and use Sourcegraph instead.
The only acceptable use of Grep/Glob is verifying content in a file you already located via Sourcegraph.

---

Trace the Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) from its gRPC service definition to containerd's implementation

The Kubernetes CRI defines a gRPC RuntimeService in its api.proto file. Trace the complete interface contract:
1. Find the CRI RuntimeService gRPC definition in the kubernetes repo (under staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/)
2. Identify the key RPC methods (RunPodSandbox, StopPodSandbox, RemovePodSandbox, etc.)
3. Find where containerd implements these CRI methods
4. Document how kubernetes vendors containerd's API types (check kubernetes/vendor/github.com/containerd/)

Your analysis must span both the kubernetes and containerd source trees under /ccb_crossrepo/src/.
Write your findings to REASONING.md in the workspace.

74-assistanttext-
I've completed the analysis and written the findings to `/workspace/REASONING.md`. Here's a summary of the key findings:

## Summary

**1. CRI RuntimeService Definition** (kubernetes repo)
- Located at `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`
- Defines two gRPC services: `RuntimeService` and `ImageService`
- Package: `runtime.v1` with Go package `k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1`

**2. Key RPC Methods Identified**
- **Pod Sandbox**: `RunPodSandbox`, `StopPodSandbox`, `RemovePodSandbox`, `PodSandboxStatus`, `ListPodSandbox`
- **Container**: `CreateContainer`, `StartContainer`, `StopContainer`, `RemoveContainer`, `ListContainers`, `ContainerStatus`, `UpdateContainerResources`
- **Execution**: `ExecSync`, `Exec`, `Attach`, `PortForward`
- **Stats/Metrics**: `ContainerStats`, `ListContainerStats`, `PodSandboxStats`, `ListPodSandboxStats`, `ListMetricDescriptors`, `ListPodSandboxMetrics`

**3. containerd's CRI Implementation**
- Core implementation in `internal/cri/server/`
- `criService` struct (`service.go:113-166`) embeds `runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer`
- Method implementations:
  - `sandbox_run.go:51-53` - `RunPodSandbox`
  - `sandbox_stop.go:33-58` - `StopPodSandbox` 
  - `sandbox_remove.go:32-101` - `RemovePodSandbox`
- Wrapped with instrumented service layer for tracing/logging

**4. Cross-Repository Vendoring**
- **Kubernetes vendors containerd**: `github.com/containerd/containerd/api v1.10.0` plus supporting packages (errdefs, log, ttrpc, typeurl)
- **containerd vendors Kubernetes CRI**: `k8s.io/cri-api v0.34.3` - this is the canonical direction where containerd implements the kubernetes-defined CRI interface

  "content": "# Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) to containerd Implementation Trace\n\n## Overview\n\nThis document traces the Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) from its gRPC service definition in the kubernetes repository to containerd's implementation. The CRI defines a standard interface that allows kubelet to communicate with any container runtime without needing to know its internal details.\n\n## 1. CRI RuntimeService gRPC Definition (Kubernetes)\n\n### Location\n- **Repository**: `github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes`\n- **Path**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`\n\n### Service Definition\n\nThe CRI defines two main gRPC services:\n\n```protobuf\n// Runtime service defines the public APIs for remote container runtimes\nservice RuntimeService { ... }\n\n// ImageService defines the public APIs for managing images\nservice ImageService { ... }\n```\n\nThe proto file uses:\n```protobuf\npackage runtime.v1;\noption go_package = \"k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1\";\n```\n\n## 2. Key RPC Methods in RuntimeService\n\n### Pod Sandbox Management\n| Method | Description | Source Location |\n|--------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `RunPodSandbox` | Creates and starts a pod-level sandbox. Runtimes ensure sandbox is in ready state on success. | `api.proto:28-30` |\n| `StopPodSandbox` | Stops running processes in sandbox and reclaims network resources. Idempotent. | `api.proto:31-40` |\n| `RemovePodSandbox` | Removes the sandbox. Must forcibly terminate and remove running containers. Idempotent. | `api.proto:41-45` |\n| `PodSandboxStatus` | Returns status of the PodSandbox | `api.proto:46-48` |\n| `ListPodSandbox` | Returns a list of PodSandboxes | `api.proto:49-50` |\n\n### Container Management\n| Method | Description |\n|--------|-------------|\n| `CreateContainer` | Creates a new container in specified PodSandbox |\n| `StartContainer` | Starts the container |\n| `StopContainer` | Stops a running container with grace period |\n| `RemoveContainer` | Removes the container (force if running) |\n| `ListContainers` | Lists all containers by filters |\n| `ContainerStatus` | Returns status of the container |\n| `UpdateContainerResources` | Updates container resources synchronously |\n| `ReopenContainerLog` | Reopens stdout/stderr log file |\n\n### Execution & Streaming\n| Method | Description |\n|--------|-------------|\n| `ExecSync` | Runs a command in container synchronously |\n| `Exec` | Prepares streaming endpoint to execute command |\n| `Attach` | Prepares streaming endpoint to attach to container |\n| `PortForward` | Prepares streaming endpoint to forward ports |\n\n### Stats & Metrics\n| Method | Description |\n|--------|-------------|\n| `ContainerStats` | Returns stats of the container |\n| `ListContainerStats` | Returns stats of all running containers |\n| `PodSandboxStats` | Returns stats of the pod sandbox |\n| `ListPodSandboxStats` | Returns stats of pod sandboxes matching filter |\n| `ListMetricDescriptors` | Gets descriptors for metrics |\n| `ListPodSandboxMetrics` | Gets pod sandbox metrics |\n\n### Runtime Configuration\n| Method | Description |\n|--------|-------------|\n| `Version` | Returns runtime name, version, and API version |\n| `UpdateRuntimeConfig` | Updates runtime configuration |\n| `Status` | Returns status of the runtime |\n| `RuntimeConfig` | Returns configuration information |\n| `CheckpointContainer` | Checkpoints a container |\n| `GetContainerEvents` | Gets container events (streaming) |\n\n## 3. containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### Implementation Architecture\n\ncontainerd implements the CRI within its `internal/cri/` package structure:\n\n```\ngithub.com/containerd/containerd/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 internal/cri/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 server/              # Main CRI server implementation\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 service.go       # criService struct definition\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 sandbox_run.go   # RunPodSandbox implementation\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 Container operations\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 ...\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 instrument/          # Instrumented service wrapper\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 instrumented_service.go\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 store/               # State stores\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 sandbox/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 container/\n\u2502   \u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 image/\n\u2502   \u2514\u2500\u2500 config/              # CRI configuration\n```\n\n### Core Implementation Type\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/service.go:113-166`\n\n```go\n// criService implements CRIService.\ntype criService struct {\n    runtime.UnimplementedRuntimeServiceServer\n    runtime.UnimplementedImageServiceServer\n\n    RuntimeService\n    ImageService\n    // config contains all configurations.\n    config criconfig.Config\n    // os is an interface for all required os operations.\n    os osinterface.OS\n    // sandboxStore stores all resources associated with sandboxes.\n    sandboxStore *sandboxstore.Store\n    // sandboxNameIndex stores all sandbox names and make sure each name is unique.\n    sandboxNameIndex *registrar.Registrar\n    // containerStore stores all resources associated with containers.\n    containerStore *containerstore.Store\n    // containerNameIndex stores all container names and make sure each name is unique.\n    containerNameIndex *registrar.Registrar\n    // netPlugin is used to setup and teardown network when run/stop pod sandbox.\n    netPlugin map[string]cni.CNI\n    // client is an instance of the containerd client\n    client *containerd.Client\n    // streamServer is the streaming server serves container streaming request.\n    streamServer streaming.Server\n    // eventMonitor is the monitor monitors containerd events.\n    eventMonitor *events.EventMonitor\n    // ... more fields\n}\n```\n\n### Method Implementations\n\n#### RunPodSandbox\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_run.go:51-53`\n\n```go\n// RunPodSandbox creates and starts a pod-level sandbox. Runtimes should ensure\n// the sandbox is in ready state.\nfunc (c *criService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (_ *runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, retErr error) {\n    // Implementation creates:\n    // 1. Unique ID and name for sandbox\n    // 2. Reserves the sandbox name\n    // 3. Creates lease for sandbox resources\n    // 4. Gets OCI runtime configuration\n    // 5. Creates sandbox store entry\n    // 6. Starts sandbox via sandboxService\n}\n```\n\n#### StopPodSandbox\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_stop.go:33-58`\n\n```go\n// StopPodSandbox stops the sandbox. If there are any running containers in the\n// sandbox, they should be forcibly terminated.\nfunc (c *criService) StopPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.StopPodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.StopPodSandboxResponse, error) {\n    // Implementation:\n    // 1. Looks up sandbox from store\n    // 2. Returns success if sandbox already removed (idempotent)\n    // 3. Forcibly stops all containers in sandbox\n    // 4. Stops sandbox via sandboxService\n}\n```\n\n#### RemovePodSandbox\n**File**: `internal/cri/server/sandbox_remove.go:32-101`\n\n```go\n// RemovePodSandbox removes the sandbox. If there are running containers in the\n// sandbox, they should be forcibly removed.\nfunc (c *criService) RemovePodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RemovePodSandboxRequest) (*runtime.RemovePodSandboxResponse, error) {\n    // Implementation:\n    // 1. Looks up sandbox from store\n    // 2. Returns success if sandbox not found (idempotent)\n    // 3. Forcibly stops sandbox\n    // 4. Deletes lease\n    // 5. Verifies network namespace is closed\n    // 6. Removes all containers in sandbox\n    // 7. Shuts down sandbox via sandboxService\n    // 8. Sends CONTAINER_DELETED event\n}\n```\n\n### Instrumented Service Wrapper\n\n**File**: `internal/cri/instrument/instrumented_service.go`\n\ncontainerd wraps the criService with instrumentation for tracing and logging:\n\n```go\nfunc (in *instrumentedService) RunPodSandbox(ctx context.Context, r *runtime.RunPodSandboxRequest) (res *runtime.RunPodSandboxResponse, err error) {\n    if err := in.checkInitialized(); err != nil {\n        return nil, err\n    }\n    span := tracing.SpanFromContext(ctx)\n    log.G(ctx).Infof(\"RunPodSandbox for %+v\", r.GetConfig().GetMetadata())\n    defer func() {\n        // ... logging and error handling\n    }()\n    res, err = in.c.RunPodSandbox(ctrdutil.WithNamespace(ctx), r)\n    return res, errgrpc.ToGRPC(err)\n}\n```\n\n## 4. 6. Key Observations\n\n1. **CRI is Kubernetes-Owned**: The CRI specification lives in `k8s.io/cri-api` within the kubernetes staging area. It defines the contract that all container runtimes must implement.\n\n2. **containerd as CRI Implementer**: containerd vendors the CRI API and provides a complete implementation in `internal/cri/server/`. The implementation uses:\n   - `sandboxStore` for sandbox state management\n   - `containerStore` for container state management\n   - `sandboxService` for actual sandbox lifecycle operations\n   - CNI plugins for network setup/teardown\n\n3. **Bidirectional Vendoring**:\n   - containerd vendors `k8s.io/cri-api` to implement the CRI\n   - Kubernetes vendors `github.com/containerd/containerd/api` for low-level containerd API access (used in testing and some runtime adapters)\n\n4. **Idempotency Contract**: The CRI explicitly requires `StopPodSandbox` and `RemovePodSandbox` to be idempotent - they must not return errors if resources are already cleaned up.\n\n5. **Instrumentation Layer**: containerd wraps its CRI implementation with an instrumented service layer that adds tracing, logging, and initialization checks to every CRI call.\n",
  "file_path": "/workspace/REASONING.md"

  "content": "# Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) to containerd Implementation Trace\n\n## Overview\n\nThis document traces the Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) from its gRPC service definition in the kubernetes repository to containerd's implementation. The CRI defines a standard interface that allows kubelet to communicate with any container runtime without needing to know its internal details.\n\n## 1. CRI RuntimeService gRPC Definition (Kubernetes)\n\n### Location\n- **Repository**: `github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes`\n- **Path**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`\n\n### Service Definition\n\nThe CRI defines two main gRPC services:\n\n```protobuf\n// Runtime service defines the public APIs for remote container runtimes\nservice RuntimeService { ... }\n\n// ImageService defines the public APIs for managing images\nservice ImageService { ... }\n```\n\nThe proto file uses:\n```protobuf\npackage runtime.v1;\noption go_package = \"k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1\";\n```\n\n## 2. Key RPC Methods in RuntimeService\n\n### Pod Sandbox Management\n| Method | Description | Source Location |\n|--------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `RunPodSandbox` | Creates and starts a pod-level sandbox. Runtimes ensure sandbox is in ready state on success. | `api.proto:28-30` |\n| `StopPodSandbox` | Stops running processes in sandbox and reclaims network resources. Idempotent. | `api.proto:31-40` |\n| `RemovePodSandbox` | Removes the sandbox. Must forcibly terminate and remove running containers. Idempotent. | `api.proto:41-45` |\n| `PodSandboxStatus` | Returns status of the PodSandbox | `api.proto:46-48` |\n| `ListPodSandbox` | Returns a list of PodSandboxes | `api.proto:49-50` |\n\n### Container Management\n| Method | Description |\n|--------|-------------|\n| `CreateContainer` | Creates a new container in specified PodSandbox |\n| `StartContainer` | Starts the container |\n| `StopContainer` | Stops a running container with grace period |\n| `RemoveContainer` | Removes the container (force if running) |\n| `ListContainers` | Lists all containers by filters |\n| `ContainerStatus` | Returns status of the container |\n| `UpdateContainerResources` | Updates container resources synchronously |\n| `ReopenContainerLog` | Reopens stdout/stderr log file |\n\n### Execution & Streaming\n| Method | Description |\n|--------|-------------|\n| `ExecSync` | Runs a command in container synchronously |\n| `Exec` | Prepares streaming endpoint to execute command |\n| `Attach` | Prepares streaming endpoint to attach to container |\n| `PortForward` | Prepares streaming endpoint to forward ports |\n\n### Stats & Metrics\n| Method | Description |\n|--------|-------------|\n| `ContainerStats` | Returns stats of the container |\n| `ListContainerStats` | Returns stats of all running containers |\n| `PodSandboxStats` | Returns stats of the pod sandbox |\n| `ListPodSandboxStats` | Returns stats of pod sandboxes matching filter |\n| `ListMetricDescriptors` | Gets descriptors for metrics |\n| `ListPodSandboxMetrics` | Gets pod sandbox metrics |\n\n### Runtime Configuration\n| Method | Description |\n|--------|-------------|\n| `Version` | Returns runtime name, version, and API version |\n| `UpdateRuntimeConfig` | Updates runtime configuration |\n| `Status` | Returns status of the runtime |\n| `RuntimeConfig` | Returns configuration information |\n| `CheckpointContainer` | Checkpoints a container |\n| `GetContainerEvents` | Gets container events (streaming) |\n\n## 3. containerd's CRI Implementation\n\n### Implementation Architecture\n\ncontainerd implements the CRI within its `internal/cri/` package structure:\n\n```\ngithub.com/containerd/containerd/\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 internal/cri/\n\u2502   \u251c\u2500\u2500 server/              # Main CRI server implementation\n\u2502   \u2502 6. Key Observations\n\n1. **CRI is Kubernetes-Owned**: The CRI specification lives in `k8s.io/cri-api` within the kubernetes staging area. It defines the contract that all container runtimes must implement.\n\n2. **containerd as CRI Implementer**: containerd vendors the CRI API and provides a complete implementation in `internal/cri/server/`. The implementation uses:\n   - `sandboxStore` for sandbox state management\n   - `containerStore` for container state management\n   - `sandboxService` for actual sandbox lifecycle operations\n   - CNI plugins for network setup/teardown\n\n3. **Bidirectional Vendoring**:\n   - containerd vendors `k8s.io/cri-api` to implement the CRI\n   - Kubernetes vendors `github.com/containerd/containerd/api` for low-level containerd API access (used in testing and some runtime adapters)\n\n4. **Idempotency Contract**: The CRI explicitly requires `StopPodSandbox` and `RemovePodSandbox` to be idempotent - they must not return errors if resources are already cleaned up.\n\n5. **Instrumentation Layer**: containerd wraps its CRI implementation with an instrumented service layer that adds tracing, logging, and initialization checks to every CRI call.\n",

# Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) to containerd Implementation Trace

## Overview

This document traces the Kubernetes Container Runtime Interface (CRI) from its gRPC service definition in the kubernetes repository to containerd's implementation. The CRI defines a standard interface that allows kubelet to communicate with any container runtime without needing to know its internal details.

## 1. CRI RuntimeService gRPC Definition (Kubernetes)

### Location
- **Repository**: `github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes`
- **Path**: `staging/src/k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1/api.proto`

### Service Definition

The CRI defines two main gRPC services:

```protobuf
// Runtime service defines the public APIs for remote container runtimes
service RuntimeService { ... }

// ImageService defines the public APIs for managing images
service ImageService { ... }
```

The proto file uses:
```protobuf
package runtime.v1;
option go_package = "k8s.io/cri-api/pkg/apis/runtime/v1";
```

## 2. Key RPC Methods in RuntimeService

### Pod Sandbox Management
| Method | Description | Source Location |
|--------|-------------|-----------------|
| `RunPodSandbox` | Creates and starts a pod-level sandbox. Runtimes ensure sandbox is in ready state on success. | `api.proto:28-30` |
| `StopPodSandbox` | Stops running processes in sandbox and reclaims network resources. Idempotent. | `api.proto:31-40` |
| `RemovePodSandbox` | Removes the sandbox. Must forcibly terminate and remove running containers. Idempotent. | `api.proto:41-45` |
| `PodSandboxStatus` | Returns status of the PodSandbox | `api.proto:46-48` |
| `ListPodSandbox` | Returns a list of PodSandboxes | `api.proto:49-50` |

### Container Management
| Method | Description |
|--------|-------------|
| `CreateContainer` | Creates a new 
... (truncated)
